     9	namespace BootstrapBlazor.Components;
    10	
    11	/// <summary>
    12	/// <para lang="zh">动态元素组件</para>
    13	/// <para lang="en">Dynamic element component</para>
    14	/// </summary>
    15	public class DynamicElement : BootstrapComponentBase, IAsyncDisposable
    16	{
    17	    /// <summary>
    18	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 TagName 属性 默认为 div</para>
    19	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the TagName property. Default is div</para>
    20	    /// </summary>
    21	    [Parameter]
    22	    [NotNull]
    23	    public string? TagName { get; set; } = "div";
    24	
    25	    /// <summary>
    26	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 Click 事件 默认 true</para>

    31	
    32	    /// <summary>
    33	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否阻止默认行为 默认 false</para>
    34	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to prevent default behavior. Default is false</para>
    35	    /// </summary>
    36	    [Parameter]
    37	    public bool PreventDefault { get; set; }
    38	
    39	    /// <summary>
    40	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否事件冒泡 默认为 false</para>
    41	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to stop event propagation. Default is false</para>
    42	    /// </summary>
    43	    [Parameter]
    44	    public bool StopPropagation { get; set; }
    45	
    46	    /// <summary>
    47	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 Click 回调委托</para>
    48	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the Click callback delegate</para>
    49	    /// </summary>
    50	    [Parameter]
    51	    public Func<Task>? OnClick { get; set; }
    52	
    53	    /// <summary>
    54	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 DoubleClick 事件 默认 true</para>
    55	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger DoubleClick event. Default is true</para>
    56	    /// </summary>
    57	    [Parameter]
    58	    public bool TriggerDoubleClick { get; set; } = true;
    59	
    60	    /// <summary>
    61	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 DoubleClick 回调委托</para>
    62	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the DoubleClick callback delegate</para>
    63	    /// </summary>
    64	    [Parameter]
    65	    public Func<Task>? OnDoubleClick { get; set; }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 OnContextMenu 回调委托</para>
    69	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the OnContextMenu callback delegate</para>
    70	    /// </summary>
    71	    [Parameter]
    72	    public Func<MouseEventArgs, Task>? OnContextMenu { get; set; }
    73	
    74	    /// <summary>
    75	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 OnContextMenu 事件 默认 false</para>
    76	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger OnContextMenu event. Default is false</para>
    77	    /// </summary>
    78	    [Parameter]
    79	    public bool TriggerContextMenu { get; set; }
    80	
    81	    /// <summary>
    82	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 内容组件</para>
    83	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the child content</para>
    84	    /// </summary>
    85	    [Parameter]
    86	    public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    87	
    88	    /// <summary>
    89	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否生成指定 Tag 元素 默认 true 生成</para>
    90	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to generate the specified Tag element. Default is true</para>
    91	    /// </summary>
    92	    [Parameter]
    93	    public bool GenerateElement { get; set; } = true;
    94	
    95	    /// <summary>
    96	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 元素唯一标识 Key 默认 null</para>
    97	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the unique key of the element. Default null</para>
    98	    /// </summary>
    99	    [Parameter]
   100	    public object? Key { get; set; }
   101	
   102	    /// <summary>
   103	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   104	    /// </summary>
   105	    /// <param name="builder"></param>
   106	    protected override void BuildRenderTree(RenderTreeBuilder builder)
   107	    {
   108	        if (GenerateElement || IsTriggerClick() || IsTriggerDoubleClick())
   109	        {
   110	            builder.OpenElement(0, TagName);
   111	
   112	            if (Key != null)
   113	            {
   114	                builder.SetKey(Key);
   115	            }
   116	            if (AdditionalAttributes != null)
   117	            {
   118	                builder.AddMultipleAttributes(1, AdditionalAttributes);
   119	            }
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        if (IsTriggerClick())
   123	        {
   124	            builder.AddAttribute(2, "onclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerClick));
   125	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(3, "onclick", PreventDefault);
   126	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(4, "onclick", StopPropagation);
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        if (IsTriggerDoubleClick())
   130	        {
   131	            builder.AddAttribute(5, "ondblclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerDoubleClick));
   132	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(6, "ondblclick", PreventDefault);
   133	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(7, "ondblclick", StopPropagation);
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        if (IsTriggerContextMenu())
   137	        {
   138	            builder.AddAttribute(8, "oncontextmenu", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerContextMenu));
   139	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(9, "oncontextmenu", true);
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        builder.AddContent(10, ChildContent);
   143	
   144	        if (GenerateElement || IsTriggerClick() || IsTriggerDoubleClick())
   145	        {
   146	            builder.CloseElement();
   147	        }
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    private bool IsTriggerClick() => TriggerClick && OnClick != null;
   151	
   152	    private bool IsTriggerDoubleClick() => TriggerDoubleClick && OnDoubleClick != null;
   153	
   154	    private bool IsTriggerContextMenu() => TriggerContextMenu && OnContextMenu != null;
   155	
   156	    private async Task OnTriggerClick()
   157	    {
   158	        if (OnClick != null)
   159	        {
   160	            await OnClick();
   161	        }
   162	    }
   163	
   164	    private async Task OnTriggerDoubleClick()
   165	    {
   166	        if (OnDoubleClick != null)
   167	        {
   168	            await OnDoubleClick();
   169	        }
   170	    }
   171	
   172	    private async Task OnTriggerContextMenu(MouseEventArgs e)
   173	    {
   174	        if (OnContextMenu != null)
   175	        {
   176	            await OnContextMenu(e);
   177	        }
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    /// <summary>
   181	    /// <para lang="zh">异步释放资源</para>
   182	    /// <para lang="en">Performs application-defined tasks associated with freeing, releasing, or resetting unmanaged resources asynchronously</para>
   183	    /// </summary>
   184	    /// <param name="disposing"></param>
   185	    protected virtual async ValueTask DisposeAsync(bool disposing)
   186	    {
   187	        if (disposing)
   188	        {
   189	            OnClick = null;
   190	            OnDoubleClick = null;
   191	            OnContextMenu = null;
   192	            ChildContent = null;
   193	        }
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    /// <summary>
   197	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   198	    /// </summary>
   199	    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
   200	    {
   201	        await DisposeAsync(true);
   202	        GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   203	    }
   204	}

    39	    /// <summary>
    40	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否事件冒泡 默认为 false</para>
    41	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to stop event propagation. Default is false</para>
    42	    /// </summary>
    43	    [Parameter]
    44	    public bool StopPropagation { get; set; }
    45	
    46	    /// <summary>
    47	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 Click 回调委托</para>
    48	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the Click callback delegate</para>
    49	    /// </summary>
    50	    [Parameter]
    51	    public Func<Task>? OnClick { get; set; }
    52	
    53	    /// <summary>
    54	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 DoubleClick 事件 默认 true</para>
    55	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger DoubleClick event. Default is true</para>
    56	    /// </summary>
    57	    [Parameter]
    58	    public bool TriggerDoubleClick { get; set; } = true;
    59	
    60	    /// <summary>
    61	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 DoubleClick 回调委托</para>
    62	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the DoubleClick callback delegate</para>
    63	    /// </summary>
    64	    [Parameter]
    65	    public Func<Task>? OnDoubleClick { get; set; }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 OnContextMenu 回调委托</para>
    69	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the OnContextMenu callback delegate</para>
    70	    /// </summary>
    71	    [Parameter]
    72	    public Func<MouseEventArgs, Task>? OnContextMenu { get; set; }
    73	
    74	    /// <summary>
    75	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 OnContextMenu 事件 默认 false</para>
    76	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger OnContextMenu event. Default is false</para>
    77	    /// </summary>
    78	    [Parameter]
    79	    public bool TriggerContextMenu { get; set; }
    80	
    81	    /// <summary>
    82	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 内容组件</para>
    83	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the child content</para>
    84	    /// </summary>
    85	    [Parameter]
    86	    public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    87	
    88	    /// <summary>
    89	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否生成指定 Tag 元素 默认 true 生成</para>
    90	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to generate the specified Tag element. Default is true</para>
    91	    /// </summary>
    92	    [Parameter]
    93	    public bool GenerateElement { get; set; } = true;
    94	
    95	    /// <summary>
    96	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 元素唯一标识 Key 默认 null</para>
    97	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the unique key of the element. Default null</para>
    98	    /// </summary>
    99	    [Parameter]
   100	    public object? Key { get; set; }
   101	
   102	    /// <summary>
   103	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   104	    /// </summary>
   105	    /// <param name="builder"></param>
   106	    protected override void BuildRenderTree(RenderTreeBuilder builder)
   107	    {
   108	        if (GenerateElement || IsTriggerClick() || IsTriggerDoubleClick())
   109	        {
   110	            builder.OpenElement(0, TagName);
   111	
   112	            if (Key != null)
   113	            {
   114	                builder.SetKey(Key);
   115	            }
   116	            if (AdditionalAttributes != null)
   117	            {
   118	                builder.AddMultipleAttributes(1, AdditionalAttributes);
   119	            }
   120	        }
   121	
   122	        if (IsTriggerClick())
   123	        {
   124	            builder.AddAttribute(2, "onclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerClick));
   125	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(3, "onclick", PreventDefault);
   126	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(4, "onclick", StopPropagation);
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        if (IsTriggerDoubleClick())
   130	        {
   131	            builder.AddAttribute(5, "ondblclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerDoubleClick));
   132	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(6, "ondblclick", PreventDefault);
   133	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(7, "ondblclick", StopPropagation);
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        if (IsTriggerContextMenu())
   137	        {
   138	            builder.AddAttribute(8, "oncontextmenu", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerContextMenu));
   139	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(9, "oncontextmenu", true);
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        builder.AddContent(10, ChildContent);
   143	
   144	        if (GenerateElement || IsTriggerClick() || IsTriggerDoubleClick())
   145	        {
   146	            builder.CloseElement();
   147	        }
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    private bool IsTriggerClick() => TriggerClick && OnClick != null;
   151	
   152	    private bool IsTriggerDoubleClick() => TriggerDoubleClick && OnDoubleClick != null;
   153	
   154	    private bool IsTriggerContextMenu() => TriggerContextMenu && OnContextMenu != null;
   155	
   156	    private async Task OnTriggerClick()
   157	    {
   158	        if (OnClick != null)
   159	        {
   160	            await OnClick();
   161	        }
   162	    }
   163	
   164	    private async Task OnTriggerDoubleClick()
   165	    {
   166	        if (OnDoubleClick != null)
   167	        {
   168	            await OnDoubleClick();
   169	        }
   170	    }
   171	
   172	    private async Task OnTriggerContextMenu(MouseEventArgs e)
   173	    {
   174	        if (OnContextMenu != null)
   175	        {
   176	            await OnContextMenu(e);
   177	        }
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    /// <summary>
   181	    /// <para lang="zh">异步释放资源</para>
   182	    /// <para lang="en">Performs application-defined tasks associated with freeing, releasing, or resetting unmanaged resources asynchronously</para>
   183	    /// </summary>
   184	    /// <param name="disposing"></param>
   185	    protected virtual async ValueTask DisposeAsync(bool disposing)
   186	    {
   187	        if (disposing)
   188	        {
   189	            OnClick = null;
   190	            OnDoubleClick = null;
   191	            OnContextMenu = null;
   192	            ChildContent = null;
   193	        }
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    /// <summary>
   197	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   198	    /// </summary>
   199	    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
   200	    {
   201	        await DisposeAsync(true);
   202	        GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   203	    }
   204	}

     8	namespace BootstrapBlazor.Components;

    10	/// <summary>
    11	/// <para lang="zh">Bootstrap Blazor 组件基类</para>
    12	/// <para lang="en">Bootstrap Blazor component base class</para>
    13	/// </summary>
    14	public abstract class BootstrapComponentBase : ComponentBase, IHandleEvent
    15	{
    16	    /// <summary>
    17	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 用户自定义属性</para>
    18	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets user defined attributes</para>
    19	    /// </summary>
    20	    [Parameter(CaptureUnmatchedValues = true)]
    21	    [JsonIgnore]
    22	    public IDictionary<string, object>? AdditionalAttributes { get; set; }
    23	
    24	    /// <summary>
    25	    /// <para lang="zh">异常捕获组件</para>
    26	    /// <para lang="en">Exception handling component</para>
    27	    /// </summary>
    28	    [CascadingParameter]
    29	    protected IErrorLogger? ErrorLogger { get; set; }
    30	
    31	    /// <summary>
    32	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 IJSRuntime 实例</para>
    33	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets IJSRuntime instance</para>
    34	    /// </summary>
    35	    [Inject]
    36	    [NotNull]
    37	    protected IJSRuntime? JSRuntime { get; set; }
    38	
    39	    /// <summary>
    40	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否需要 Render 组件 默认 false 需要重新渲染组件</para>
    41	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to render the component. Default is false (re-render required)</para>
    42	    /// </summary>
    43	    protected bool IsNotRender { get; set; }
    44	
    45	    [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
    46	    private async Task CallStateHasChangedOnAsyncCompletion(Task task)
    47	    {
    48	        try
    49	        {
    50	            await task;
    51	        }
    52	        catch (Exception ex) // avoiding exception filters for AOT runtime support
    53	        {
    54	            // Ignore exceptions from task cancellations, but don't bother issuing a state change.
    55	            if (task.IsCanceled)
    56	            {
    57	                return;
    58	            }
    59	
    60	            if (ErrorLogger is { EnableErrorLogger: true })
    61	            {
    62	                IsNotRender = true;
    63	                await ErrorLogger.HandlerExceptionAsync(ex);
    64	            }
    65	            else
    66	            {
    67	                // 未开启全局捕获
    68	                throw;
    69	            }
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        if (!IsNotRender)
    73	        {
    74	            StateHasChanged();
    75	        }
    76	        else
    77	        {
    78	            IsNotRender = false;
    79	        }
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    Task IHandleEvent.HandleEventAsync(EventCallbackWorkItem callback, object? arg)
    83	    {
    84	        var task = callback.InvokeAsync(arg);
    85	        var shouldAwaitTask = task.Status != TaskStatus.RanToCompletion &&
    86	            task.Status != TaskStatus.Canceled;
    87	
    88	        if (!IsNotRender)
    89	        {
    90	            // After each event, we synchronously re-render (unless !ShouldRender())
    91	            // This just saves the developer the trouble of putting "StateHasChanged();"
    92	            // at the end of every event callback.
    93	            StateHasChanged();
    94	        }
    95	        else
    96	        {
    97	            IsNotRender = false;
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        return shouldAwaitTask ?
   101	            CallStateHasChangedOnAsyncCompletion(task) :
   102	            Task.CompletedTask;
   103	    }
   104	}

    44	    public bool StopPropagation { get; set; }

    46	    /// <summary>
    47	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 Click 回调委托</para>
    48	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the Click callback delegate</para>
    49	    /// </summary>
    50	    [Parameter]
    51	    public Func<Task>? OnClick { get; set; }
    52	
    53	    /// <summary>
    54	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 DoubleClick 事件 默认 true</para>
    55	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger DoubleClick event. Default is true</para>
    56	    /// </summary>
    57	    [Parameter]
    58	    public bool TriggerDoubleClick { get; set; } = true;
    59	
    60	    /// <summary>
    61	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 DoubleClick 回调委托</para>
    62	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the DoubleClick callback delegate</para>
    63	    /// </summary>
    64	    [Parameter]
    65	    public Func<Task>? OnDoubleClick { get; set; }
    66	
    67	    /// <summary>
    68	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 OnContextMenu 回调委托</para>
    69	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the OnContextMenu callback delegate</para>
    70	    /// </summary>
    71	    [Parameter]
    72	    public Func<MouseEventArgs, Task>? OnContextMenu { get; set; }

   100	    public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
   101	
   102	    /// <summary>
   103	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否生成指定 Tag 元素 默认 true 生成</para>
   104	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to generate the specified Tag element. Default is true</para>
   105	    /// </summary>
   106	    [Parameter]
   107	    public bool GenerateElement { get; set; } = true;
   108	
   109	    /// <summary>
   110	    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 元素唯一标识 Key 默认 null</para>
   111	    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the unique key of the element. Default null</para>
   112	    /// </summary>
   113	    [Parameter]
   114	    public object? Key { get; set; }
   115	
   116	    /// <summary>
   117	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   118	    /// </summary>
   119	    /// <param name="builder"></param>
   120	    protected override void BuildRenderTree(RenderTreeBuilder builder)
   121	    {
   122	        if (IsGenerateElement())
   123	        {
   124	            builder.OpenElement(0, TagName);
   125	
   126	            if (Key != null)
   127	            {
   128	                builder.SetKey(Key);
   129	            }
   130	            if (AdditionalAttributes != null)
   131	            {
   132	                builder.AddMultipleAttributes(1, AdditionalAttributes);
   133	            }
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        if (IsTriggerClick())
   137	        {
   138	            builder.AddAttribute(2, "onclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerClick));
   139	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(3, "onclick", PreventDefault);
   140	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(4, "onclick", StopPropagation);
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        if (IsTriggerDoubleClick())
   144	        {
   145	            builder.AddAttribute(5, "ondblclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerDoubleClick));
   146	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(6, "ondblclick", PreventDefault);
   147	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(7, "ondblclick", StopPropagation);
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        if (IsTriggerContextMenu())
   151	        {
   152	            builder.AddAttribute(8, "oncontextmenu", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerContextMenu));
   153	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(9, "oncontextmenu", true);
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        if (IsTriggerTouchStart())
   157	        {
   158	            builder.AddAttribute(10, "ontouchstart", EventCallback.Factory.Create<TouchEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerTouchStart));
   159	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(11, "ontouchstart", PreventDefault);
   160	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(12, "ontouchstart", StopPropagation);
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        if (IsTriggerTouchEnd())
   164	        {
   165	            builder.AddAttribute(13, "ontouchend", EventCallback.Factory.Create<TouchEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerTouchEnd));
   166	            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(14, "ontouchend", PreventDefault);
   167	            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(15, "ontouchend", StopPropagation);
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        builder.AddContent(16, ChildContent);
   171	
   172	        if (IsGenerateElement())
   173	        {
   174	            builder.CloseElement();
   175	        }
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    private bool IsGenerateElement() => GenerateElement || IsTriggerClick() || IsTriggerDoubleClick() || IsTriggerContextMenu() || IsTriggerTouchStart() || IsTriggerTouchEnd();
   179	
   180	    private bool IsTriggerClick() => TriggerClick && OnClick != null;
   181	
   182	    private bool IsTriggerDoubleClick() => TriggerDoubleClick && OnDoubleClick != null;
   183	
   184	    private bool IsTriggerContextMenu() => TriggerContextMenu && OnContextMenu != null;
   185	
   186	    private bool IsTriggerTouchStart() => OnTouchStart != null;
   187	
   188	    private bool IsTriggerTouchEnd() => OnTouchEnd != null;
   189	
   190	    private async Task OnTriggerClick()
   191	    {
   192	        if (OnClick != null)
   193	        {
   194	            await OnClick();
   195	        }
   196	    }
   197	
   198	    private async Task OnTriggerDoubleClick()
   199	    {
   200	        if (OnDoubleClick != null)
   201	        {
   202	            await OnDoubleClick();
   203	        }
   204	    }
   205	
   206	    private async Task OnTriggerContextMenu(MouseEventArgs e)
   207	    {
   208	        if (OnContextMenu != null)
   209	        {
   210	            await OnContextMenu(e);
   211	        }
   212	    }
   213	}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Rendering;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Web;

namespace BootstrapBlazor.Components;

/// <summary>
/// <para lang="zh">动态元素组件</para>
/// <para lang="en">Dynamic element component</para>
/// </summary>
public class DynamicElement : BootstrapComponentBase
{
    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 TagName 属性 默认为 div</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the TagName property. Default is div</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    [NotNull]
    public string? TagName { get; set; } = "div";

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 Click 事件 默认 true</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger Click event. Default is true</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public bool TriggerClick { get; set; } = true;

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否阻止默认行为 默认 false</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to prevent default behavior. Default is false</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public bool PreventDefault { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否事件冒泡 默认为 false</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to stop event propagation. Default is false</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public bool StopPropagation { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 Click 回调委托</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the Click callback delegate</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public Func<Task>? OnClick { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 DoubleClick 事件 默认 true</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger DoubleClick event. Default is true</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public bool TriggerDoubleClick { get; set; } = true;

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 DoubleClick 回调委托</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the DoubleClick callback delegate</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public Func<Task>? OnDoubleClick { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 OnContextMenu 回调委托</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the OnContextMenu callback delegate</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public Func<MouseEventArgs, Task>? OnContextMenu { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否触发 OnContextMenu 事件 默认 false</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to trigger OnContextMenu event. Default is false</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public bool TriggerContextMenu { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 TouchStart 回调委托</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the TouchStart callback delegate</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public Func<TouchEventArgs, Task>? OnTouchStart { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 TouchEnd 回调委托</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the TouchEnd callback delegate</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public Func<TouchEventArgs, Task>? OnTouchEnd { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 内容组件</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the child content</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 是否生成指定 Tag 元素 默认 true 生成</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets whether to generate the specified Tag element. Default is true</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public bool GenerateElement { get; set; } = true;

    /// <summary>
    /// <para lang="zh">获得/设置 元素唯一标识 Key 默认 null</para>
    /// <para lang="en">Gets or sets the unique key of the element. Default null</para>
    /// </summary>
    [Parameter]
    public object? Key { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// <inheritdoc/>
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="builder"></param>
    protected override void BuildRenderTree(RenderTreeBuilder builder)
    {
        if (IsGenerateElement())
        {
            builder.OpenElement(0, TagName);

            if (Key != null)
            {
                builder.SetKey(Key);
            }
            if (AdditionalAttributes != null)
            {
                builder.AddMultipleAttributes(1, AdditionalAttributes);
            }
        }

        if (IsTriggerClick())
        {
            builder.AddAttribute(2, "onclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerClick));
            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(3, "onclick", PreventDefault);
            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(4, "onclick", StopPropagation);
        }

        if (IsTriggerDoubleClick())
        {
            builder.AddAttribute(5, "ondblclick", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerDoubleClick));
            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(6, "ondblclick", PreventDefault);
            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(7, "ondblclick", StopPropagation);
        }

        if (IsTriggerContextMenu())
        {
            builder.AddAttribute(8, "oncontextmenu", EventCallback.Factory.Create<MouseEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerContextMenu));
            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(9, "oncontextmenu", true);
        }

        if (IsTriggerTouchStart())
        {
            builder.AddAttribute(10, "ontouchstart", EventCallback.Factory.Create<TouchEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerTouchStart));
            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(11, "ontouchstart", PreventDefault);
            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(12, "ontouchstart", StopPropagation);
        }

        if (IsTriggerTouchEnd())
        {
            builder.AddAttribute(13, "ontouchend", EventCallback.Factory.Create<TouchEventArgs>(this, OnTriggerTouchEnd));
            builder.AddEventPreventDefaultAttribute(14, "ontouchend", PreventDefault);
            builder.AddEventStopPropagationAttribute(15, "ontouchend", StopPropagation);
        }

        builder.AddContent(16, ChildContent);

        if (IsGenerateElement())
        {
            builder.CloseElement();
        }
    }

    private bool IsGenerateElement() => GenerateElement || IsTriggerClick() || IsTriggerDoubleClick() || IsTriggerContextMenu() || IsTriggerTouchStart() || IsTriggerTouchEnd();

    private bool IsTriggerClick() => TriggerClick && OnClick != null;

    private bool IsTriggerDoubleClick() => TriggerDoubleClick && OnDoubleClick != null;

    private bool IsTriggerContextMenu() => TriggerContextMenu && OnContextMenu != null;

    private bool IsTriggerTouchStart() => OnTouchStart != null;

    private bool IsTriggerTouchEnd() => OnTouchEnd != null;

    private async Task OnTriggerClick()
    {
        if (OnClick != null)
        {
            await OnClick();
        }
    }

    private async Task OnTriggerDoubleClick()
    {
        if (OnDoubleClick != null)
        {
            await OnDoubleClick();
        }
    }

    private async Task OnTriggerContextMenu(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        if (OnContextMenu != null)
        {
            await OnContextMenu(e);
        }
    }
}
